#include <regex>
#include <iostream>

int main() {
  {
    std::regex e{"\\<\\<\\w+"};
    std::cout << std::regex_search("a ", e) << std::endl; // prints 0
  }
  {
    boost::regex e{"\\<\\<\\w+"};
    std::cout << boost::regex_search("a ", e) << std::endl; // prints 1
  }
}
